**`e232679` (M-L1-taxonomy T-6a + T-6b — ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING semantics + maxRecords cap-lift to 50000) reviewer-APPROVED 2026-04-30 **RETROACTIVELY** Phase N (PR #112 already merged into dev `e511cbc` at 23:31:57Z **without pre-merge Phase N gate** per workflow.md step 6 — process violation logged as TD-42; impl quality clean):**
- **2-commit chain on PR #112** (combined architect + registry-dev branch `feature/M-L1-T6a-tests-red`, force-pushed to combine T-6a + T-6b after force-merge): `8268067 architect@paxio.network test(M-L1-taxonomy T-6): RED tests for ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING semantics` (3 test assertions in `products/01-registry/tests/postgres-storage.test.ts` updated to express new skip-if-exists behavior) → `e232679 registry-dev@paxio.network fix(M-L1-taxonomy T-6b): skip-if-exists + maxRecords 50000` (2-file impl: `products/01-registry/app/infra/postgres-storage.ts` SQL change + dead-code removal; `products/01-registry/app/api/admin-crawl.js` cap 5000→50000).
- **Closes 2 functional gaps in M-L1 crawler pipeline**: (a) **T-6a/T-6b skip-if-exists**: previous `ON CONFLICT (did) DO UPDATE SET ...` re-wrote ALL 10 mutable fields on every cron tick — meant Smithery's first 5K records got overwritten in-place each 6h tick, never advancing; new `ON CONFLICT (did) DO NOTHING` skips silently so crawler естественно идёт «вперёд» across the full ~7K Smithery catalog in 1-2 cron ticks; secondary `SQL.updateBySourceExternalId` fallback (used when `(source, external_id)` partial-unique fired with different DID) becomes dead code under DO NOTHING semantics, correctly removed; the partial-unique 23505 path now silent-ok'd via early `return ok(undefined)` branch in catch block, preserving same skip semantics; non-uniqueness 23505 (e.g. CHECK constraint on category enum, FK violations) still surfaces via `toStorageError(e)` → `constraint_violation`. (b) **maxRecords cap-lift**: 5000 → 50000 in `admin-crawl.js::runCrawler({maxRecords: 50000})` — Smithery currently ~7K, headroom for growth without code change.
- **Substantive validation (reviewer in architect's worktree `/tmp/paxio-ml1-tax`, identity=reviewer post-switch)**: targeted `pnpm exec vitest run products/01-registry/tests/postgres-storage.test.ts` → **27/27 GREEN** ✓ (was 24/24 before T-6a 3-assertion update; +3 net for new SQL semantics); `pnpm typecheck` → 0 errors ✓; full root vitest baseline → **68 files / 1414 passed | 26 skipped | 5 todo / 1446 total** (1 failure: `tests/m-q22-reviewer-chore-coverage.test.ts` correctly flagging this very Phase N gap — 13 PR merges in last 50 dev commits without `chore(reviewer):` follow-up — confirms governance protocol works as designed). Test-files-not-modified-by-impl-author check ✓: `git diff-tree e232679 --name-only` shows only 2 impl files, no `tests/` touched. Identity-vs-scope per scope-guard table: architect@ on `tests/` ✓; registry-dev@ on `products/01-registry/{app/api,app/infra}/` ✓.
- **Quality (P0/P1/P2 walk)**: P0 — admin endpoint preserves Bearer admin-token auth + ValidationError on bad source + rate-limit 5min ✓ (multi-tenancy N/A — this is system-level admin operation, not tenant-scoped data; auth via `headers.authorization` not `body.adminDid` ✓); SQL change preserves parameterized queries (12-param `$1..$12` placeholders unchanged) ✓; no secrets in code; AppError hierarchy preserved (`errors.AuthError`, `errors.ValidationError`, `errors.InternalError`). P1 — handler format `{httpMethod, path, method}` ✓; conventional commits `test(M-L1-taxonomy T-6):` / `fix(M-L1-taxonomy T-6b):` ✓; identity matches per scope-guard table for both authors; AppError used correctly. P2 — `maxRecords: 50000` is now hardcoded magic number inline (was 5000 hardcoded magic number inline before — same hygiene posture, no regression; minor TD candidate to externalize to `app/data/*.json` per code-style.md::Data Externalization but pre-existing pattern, not introduced by this PR); `isUniqueExternalIdViolation` helper correctly removed as dead code; result-pattern preserved (`return ok(undefined)` / `return err(toStorageError(e))`).
- **Functional impact analysis**: under DO NOTHING, if Smithery later re-issues a record under a NEW DID for the same `(source, external_id)` pair (e.g. wallet rotation), storage skips silently — old DID's row stays with stale `name/description/capability/...`. This is acceptable trade-off explicit in milestone semantics («skip if exists, crawler идёт вперёд»); a separate future mechanism (manual re-crawl with --force flag, scheduled garbage collection of inactive DIDs) would handle stale-row sweep. NOT a blocker.
- **Memory consideration**: `maxRecords: 50000` may load ~50K records into memory in single crawl (current Smithery ~7K → fine; if catalog grows past ~30K could need pagination/streaming). Soft signal, not blocking. Tracked for future M-L1-T7+ if observed.

Per `frontend-rules.md::J5` — Tailwind 4 only. **However**, B5 design source (`docs/design/paxio-b5/Paxio-B5.html`) is plain HTML+CSS-vars, milestone spec defers app-level styling to M-L10.5; the inline pattern pairs cleanly with M-L10.2 CSS custom properties (`var(--ink-0)`, `var(--paper-0)`, `var(--gold)`). Treat as intentional B5 port; flag for architect to clarify if Tailwind migration is expected in M-L10.5 wiring. (N3) `Header.tsx:33` empty `try { localStorage.setItem(...) } catch {}` for quota/private-mode — common idiom, but per F5 should at minimum log via injected logger. Cosmetic. **Process / infrastructure issues (NOT impl quality, recorded as new tech-debt)**: (P1) Detached HEAD on dev's worktree — commit `2d3604e` lives on `(no branch)` in `/tmp/paxio-fd-ml103`, not on `feature/M-L10.3-shell` per spec. Same class as M-Q17 (literal `$HOME` bug). Architect-owned script bug — does NOT affect impl. **`2982b17` (M-Q17 — remove `TMPDIR` from project settings, fix literal `$HOME/` dir bug) reviewer-APPROVED 2026-04-28 — PR #76 merged to `dev` 2026-04-28:**
- PR #76 `feature/M-Q17-tmpdir-fix` (1 commit `b2f4fa3` architect, 4 files, +112/−2): self-inflicted incident self-diagnosed self-fixed. Architect's prior commit `72c2853` («TMPDIR isolation per OS user», Apr 28) added `"TMPDIR": "$HOME/.cache/paxio-tmp"` to project-level `.claude/settings.json::env` expecting Claude Code to expand `$HOME` per OS user — but Claude Code passes env values to subprocesses **literally without expansion**. Result: any tool running `mkdir -p "$TMPDIR/..."` without shell expansion creates a literal `./\$HOME/.cache/paxio-tmp/...` directory in repo root. Architect's user-level `~/.claude/settings.json` had absolute-path TMPDIR override masking the bug; only manifested for OS users without the override. **Fix scope (4 files)**: `.claude/settings.json` — `env.TMPDIR` removed, only `CLAUDE_AUTOCOMPACT_PCT_OVERRIDE: "90"` retained; `.gitignore` — defence-in-depth additions: `$HOME/` (with rationale comment), `.pi/` (Pi harness state), `.claude/{extensions,worktrees,wrappers}/` (Pi runtime); `CLAUDE.md` — new section «Per-OS-user setup — required (do once)» with absolute-path JSON template + explicit prohibition on project-level TMPDIR + M-Q17 incident reference; `tests/m-q17-tmpdir-no-literal-home.test.ts` — 6 assertions: settings has no TMPDIR key, no literal `$HOME` in env values, gitignore lists `$HOME/` + Pi runtime dirs, CLAUDE.md documents per-user setup + absolute path, CI canary checks no literal `$HOME/` dir at repo root with `skipIf(sessionHasBadTmpdir)` to protect pre-merge sessions from false-positive (sessions started before merge inherit bad TMPDIR; their vitest forks recreate `$HOME/` until restart). **Independent reproduction in review session itself**: my session's `TMPDIR=$HOME/.cache/paxio-tmp` (literal); review-worktree had `/tmp/paxio-rev-pr76/$HOME/` directory created by tools — direct empirical confirmation of architect's diagnosis. **Composes with M-Q3**: `scope-guard.md::Per-session worktree isolation` covered cross-user `node_modules/` EPERM chmod; M-Q17 closes the parallel hole for shared `/tmp` cache (gh-cli + node compile cache). Together: per-session worktree (own `node_modules/`) + per-OS-user TMPDIR (own `$TMPDIR/<gh-cli,node-compile>-cache/`). **Verification (`/tmp/paxio-rev-pr76`)**: typecheck 0 errors, vitest **1154/1186 GREEN** + 27 skipped (1 M-Q17 canary + 26 pre-existing) + 5 todo, m-q17 5 passed + 1 skipped (canary skipIf working as designed); CI all green. **Notes (non-blocking, recorded for follow-up)**: (N1) `.gitignore` rationale comment refers to `tests/m-tmpdir-no-literal-home.test.ts` but actual filename is `tests/m-q17-tmpdir-no-literal-home.test.ts` — trivial doc fix in next governance commit. ## Source Structure (фактическое)

```
paxio/
├── server/                                    # Fastify infrastructure (CommonJS)
│   ├── main.cjs                               # entry point
│   ├── src/{http,loader,logger,ws}.cjs
│   ├── lib/errors.cjs                         # ⚠ mirrors app/errors/ (TD-01)
│   └── infrastructure/                        # empty, populated M01+
├── app/                                       # Business logic (VM sandbox)
│   ├── types/                                 # architect — Result, Did, Capability, AgentCard, ErrorCode
│   ├── interfaces/                            # architect — Logger, Clock
│   ├── errors/                                # ✅ DONE (M00) — AppError hierarchy
│   ├── lib/                                   # ✅ DONE (M00) — logger.ts, clock.ts
│   ├── config/                                # empty placeholder
│   ├── data/                                  # empty placeholder
│   ├── domain/                                # empty placeholder
│   └── api/                                   # empty placeholder
├── products/
│   ├── 01-registry/
│   │   └── app/                               # ✅ DONE (M01 + M-L1-impl MVP) — TS registry core + crawler + Postgres storage
│   │       ├── api/                           # register, resolve, find, claim, count handlers
│   │       ├── domain/                        # did-gen, registry, search, claim (in-memory), crawler.ts (M-L1)
│   │       │   └── sources/                   # mcp.ts (real Smithery) + a2a/erc8004/fetch-ai/virtuals (stubs, M-L1-expansion)
│   │       └── infra/postgres-storage.ts      # Postgres AgentStorage impl (idempotent upsert, pg Pool injected)
│   ├── 02-facilitator/
│   │   └── app/                               # ✅ DONE (M-L4a) — FAP Rails Catalog (stub router)
│   │       ├── data/rails-catalog.json        # 4 rails: x402, mpp, tap, btc-l1 (share_pct: 0)
│   │       ├── domain/fap-router.ts           # createFapRouter factory + ZodRailInfo validate-once
│   │       └── api/fap-rails.js               # GET /api/fap/rails (public, no tenant filter)
│   ├── 07-intelligence/
│   │   └── app/                               # 🟡 PARTIAL (M01c + M-L4a wiring)
│   │       ├── domain/landing-stats.ts        # createLandingStats(deps) + getRailsCatalog dep
│   │       └── api/landing-*.js (×7)          # SSR + 6 polling endpoints
│   ├── 03-wallet/
│   │   └── canister/                          # ✅ DONE (M02) — Wallet Rust canister
│   │       ├── src/{lib,ecdsa,addresses,storage,types,errors}.rs
│   │       └── wallet.did                     # Candid interface
│   ├── 04-security/
│   │   └── canister/                          # ✅ DONE (M03) — Security Sidecar Intent Verifier
│   │       └── src/{lib,verifier,storage,types,errors}.rs
│   └── 06-compliance/
│       └── canisters/audit-log/               # ✅ DONE (M04) — Audit Log (SHA-256 hash chain)
│           ├── src/{lib,chain,storage,types,errors}.rs
│           └── audit_log.did                    # Candid interface
├── platform/
│   └── canister-shared/                       # ✅ DONE (M00c) — AgentId, TxHash primitives
├── Cargo.toml                                 # ROOT Rust workspace (platform/canister-shared, products/*/canister(s))
├── packages/
│   ├── sdk/                                   # @paxio/sdk skeleton
│   ├── mcp-server/                            # skeleton
│   └── frontend/                              # placeholder (M11+)
├── cli/                                       # placeholder (M14)
├── tests/                                     # 6 test files, 72 GREEN
├── scripts/                                   # verify_foundation.sh
├── docs/                                      # strategy, roadmap, FA, sprints, e2e, product-metrics
├── opensrc/                                   # pinned external refs
└── .github/workflows/ci.yml                   # stub
```
